They also stole their shoes, because their own were far too small for Crabbe- and Goyle-size feet. Then, still stunned at what they had just done, they sprinted up to Moaning MyrtleвҖҷs bathroom.
They could hardly see for the thick black smoke issuing from the stall in which Hermione was stirring the cauldron. Pulling their robes up over their faces, Harry and Ron knocked softly on the door.
вҖңHermione?вҖқ
They heard the scrape of the lock and Hermione emerged, shiny-faced and looking anxious. Behind her they heard the gloop gloop of the bubbling, glutinous potion. Three glass tumblers stood ready on the toilet seat.
вҖңDid you get them?вҖқ Hermione asked breathlessly.
Harry showed her GoyleвҖҷs hair.
вҖңGood. And I sneaked these spare robes out of the laundry,вҖқ Hermione said, holding up a small sack. вҖңYouвҖҷll need bigger sizes once youвҖҷre Crabbe and Goyle.вҖқ
The three of them stared into the cauldron. Close up, the potion looked like thick, dark mud, bubbling sluggishly.
вҖңIвҖҷm sure IвҖҷve done everything right,вҖқ said Hermione, nervously rereading the splotched page of Moste Potente Potions. вҖңIt looks like the book says it should вҖҰ once weвҖҷve drunk it, weвҖҷll have exactly an hour before we change back into ourselves.вҖқ
вҖңNow what?вҖқ Ron whispered.
вҖңWe separate it into three glasses and add the hairs.вҖқ
Hermione ladled large dollops of the potion into each of the glasses. Then, her hand trembling, she shook Millicent BulstrodeвҖҷs hair out of its bottle into the first glass.
The potion hissed loudly like a boiling kettle and frothed madly. A second later, it had turned a sick sort of yellow.
вҖңUrgh вҖ” essence of Millicent Bulstrode,вҖқ said Ron, eyeing it with loathing. вҖңBet it tastes disgusting.вҖқ
вҖңAdd yours, then,вҖқ said Hermione.
Harry dropped GoyleвҖҷs hair into the middle glass and Ron put CrabbeвҖҷs into the last one. Both glasses hissed and frothed: GoyleвҖҷs turned the khaki color of a booger, CrabbeвҖҷs a dark, murky brown.
вҖңHang on,вҖқ said Harry as Ron and Hermione reached for their glasses. вҖңWeвҖҷd better not all drink them in here. вҖҰ Once we turn into Crabbe and Goyle we wonвҖҷt fit. And Millicent BulstrodeвҖҷs no pixie.вҖқ
вҖңGood thinking,вҖқ said Ron, unlocking the door. вҖңWeвҖҷll take sepВӯarate stalls.вҖқ
Careful not to spill a drop of his Polyjuice Potion, Harry slipped into the middle stall.
вҖңReady?вҖқ he called.
вҖңReady,вҖқ came RonвҖҷs and HermioneвҖҷs voices.
вҖңOne вҖ” two вҖ” three вҖ”вҖқ
Pinching his nose, Harry drank the potion down in two large gulps. It tasted like overcooked cabbage.
Immediately, his insides started writhing as though heвҖҷd just swallowed live snakes вҖ” doubled up, he wondered whether he was going to be sick вҖ” then a burning sensation spread rapidly from his stomach to the very ends of his fingers and toes вҖ” next, bringВӯing him gasping to all fours, came a horrible melting feeling, as the skin all over his body bubbled like hot wax вҖ” and before his eyes, his hands began to grow, the fingers thickened, the nails broadened, the knuckles were bulging like bolts вҖ” his shoulders stretched painfully and a prickling on his forehead told him that hair was creeping down toward his eyebrows вҖ” his robes ripped as his chest expanded like a barrel bursting its hoops вҖ” his feet were agony in shoes four sizes too small вҖ”
As suddenly as it had started, everything stopped. Harry lay facedown on the stone-cold floor, listening to Myrtle gurgling moВӯrosely in the end toilet. With difficulty, he kicked off his shoes and stood up. So this was what it felt like, being Goyle. His large hand trembling, he pulled off his old robes, which were hanging a foot above his ankles, pulled on the spare ones, and laced up GoyleвҖҷs boatlike shoes. He reached up to brush his hair out of his eyes and met only the short growth of wiry bristles, low on his forehead. Then he realized that his glasses were clouding his eyes because Goyle obviously didnвҖҷt need them вҖ” he took them off and called, вҖңAre you two okay?вҖқ GoyleвҖҷs low rasp of a voice issued from his mouth.
вҖңYeah,вҖқ came the deep grunt of Crabbe from his right.
Harry unlocked his door and stepped in front of the cracked mirror. Goyle stared back at him out of dull, deepset eyes. Harry scratched his ear. So did Goyle.
RonвҖҷs door opened. They stared at each other. Except that he looked pale and shocked, Ron was indistinguishable from Crabbe, from the pudding-bowl haircut to the long, gorilla arms.
вҖңThis is unbelievable,вҖқ said Ron, approaching the mirror and prodding CrabbeвҖҷs flat nose. вҖңUnbelievable.вҖқ
вҖңWeвҖҷd better get going,вҖқ said Harry, loosening the watch that was cutting into GoyleвҖҷs thick wrist. вҖңWeвҖҷve still got to find out where the Slytherin common room is. I only hope we can find someone to follow вҖҰвҖқ
Ron, who had been gazing at Harry, said, вҖңYou donвҖҷt know how bizarre it is to see Goyle thinking.вҖқ He banged on HermioneвҖҷs door. вҖңCвҖҷmon, we need to go вҖ”вҖқ
A high-pitched voice answered him.
вҖңI вҖ” I donвҖҷt think IвҖҷm going to come after all. You go on withВӯout me.вҖқ
вҖңHermione, we know Millicent BulstrodeвҖҷs ugly, no oneвҖҷs going to know itвҖҷs you вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңNo вҖ” really вҖ” I donвҖҷt think IвҖҷll come. You two hurry up, youвҖҷre wasting time вҖ”вҖқ
Harry looked at Ron, bewildered.
вҖңThat looks more like Goyle,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңThatвҖҷs how he looks every time a teacher asks him a question.вҖқ
вҖңHermione, are you okay?вҖқ said Harry through the door.
вҖңFine вҖ” IвҖҷm fine вҖ” go on вҖ”вҖқ
Harry looked at his watch. Five of their precious sixty minutes had already passed.
вҖңWeвҖҷll meet you back here, all right?вҖқ he said.
Harry and Ron opened the door of the bathroom carefully, checked that the coast was clear, and set off.
вҖңDonвҖҷt swing your arms like that,вҖқ Harry muttered to Ron.
вҖңEh?вҖқ
вҖңCrabbe holds them sort of stiff. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңHowвҖҷs this?вҖқ
вҖңYeah, thatвҖҷs better. вҖҰвҖқ
They went down the marble staircase. All they needed now was a Slytherin that they could follow to the Slytherin common room, but there was nobody around.
вҖңAny ideas?вҖқ muttered Harry.
вҖңThe Slytherins always come up to breakfast from over there,вҖқ said Ron, nodding at the entrance to the dungeons. The words had barely left his mouth when a girl with long, curly hair emerged from the entrance.
вҖңExcuse me,вҖқ said Ron, hurrying up to her. вҖңWeвҖҷve forgotten the way to our common room.вҖқ
вҖңI beg your pardon?вҖқ said the girl stiffly. вҖңOur common room? IвҖҷm a Ravenclaw.вҖқ
She walked away, looking suspiciously back at them.
Harry and Ron hurried down the stone steps into the darkness, their footsteps echoing particularly loudly as CrabbeвҖҷs and GoyleвҖҷs huge feet hit the floor, feeling that this wasnвҖҷt going to be as easy as they had hoped.
The labyrinthine passages were deserted. They walked deeper and deeper under the school, constantly checking their watches to see how much time they had left. After a quarter of an hour, just when they were getting desperate, they heard a sudden movement ahead.
вҖңHa!вҖқ said Ron excitedly. вҖңThereвҖҷs one of them now!вҖқ
The figure was emerging from a side room. As they hurried nearer, however, their hearts sank. It wasnвҖҷt a Slytherin, it was Percy.
вҖңWhatвҖҷre you doing down here?вҖқ said Ron in surprise.
Percy looked affronted.
вҖңThat,вҖқ he said stiffly, вҖңis none of your business. ItвҖҷs Crabbe, isnвҖҷt it?вҖқ
вҖңWh вҖ” oh, yeah,вҖқ said Ron.
вҖңWell, get off to your dormitories,вҖқ said Percy sternly. вҖңItвҖҷs not safe to go wandering around dark corridors these days.вҖқ
вҖңYou are,вҖқ Ron pointed out.
вҖңI,вҖқ said Percy, drawing himself up, вҖңam a prefect. NothingвҖҷs about to attack me.вҖқ
A voice suddenly echoed behind Harry and Ron. Draco Malfoy was strolling toward them, and for the first time in his life, Harry was pleased to see him.
вҖңThere you are,вҖқ he drawled, looking at them. вҖңHave you two been pigging out in the Great Hall all this time? IвҖҷve been looking for you; I want to show you something really funny.вҖқ
Malfoy glanced witheringly at Percy.
вҖңAnd whatвҖҷre you doing down here, Weasley?вҖқ he sneered.
Percy looked outraged.
вҖңYou want to show a bit more respect to a school prefect!вҖқ he said. вҖңI donвҖҷt like your attitude!вҖқ
Malfoy sneered and motioned for Harry and Ron to follow him. Harry almost said something apologetic to Percy but caught himВӯself just in time. He and Ron hurried after Malfoy, who said as they turned into the next passage, вҖңThat Peter Weasley вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңPercy,вҖқ Ron corrected him automatically.
вҖңWhatever,вҖқ said Malfoy. вҖңIвҖҷve noticed him sneaking around a lot lately. And I bet I know what heвҖҷs up to. He thinks heвҖҷs going to catch SlytherinвҖҷs heir single-handed.вҖқ
He gave a short, derisive laugh. Harry and Ron exchanged exВӯcited looks.
Malfoy paused by a stretch of bare, damp stone wall.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs the new password again?вҖқ he said to Harry.
вҖңEr вҖ”вҖқ said Harry.
вҖңOh, yeah вҖ” pure-blood!вҖқ said Malfoy, not listening, and a stone door concealed in the wall slid open. Malfoy marched through it, and Harry and Ron followed him.
The Slytherin common room was a long, low underground room with rough stone walls and ceiling from which round, greenВӯish lamps were hanging on chains. A fire was crackling under an elaborately carved mantelpiece ahead of them, and several SlythВӯerins were silhouetted around it in high-backed chairs.
вҖңWait here,вҖқ said Malfoy to Harry and Ron, motioning them to a pair of empty chairs set back from the fire. вҖңIвҖҷll go and get it вҖ” my fatherвҖҷs just sent it to me вҖ”вҖқ
Wondering what Malfoy was going to show them, Harry and Ron sat down, doing their best to look at home.
Malfoy came back a minute later, holding what looked like a newspaper clipping. He thrust it under RonвҖҷs nose.
вҖңThatвҖҷll give you a laugh,вҖқ he said.
Harry saw Ron's eyes widen in shock. He read the clipping quickly, gave a very forced laugh, and handed it to Harry.
It had been clipped out of the Daily Prophet, and it said:
INQUIRY AT THE MINISTRY OF MAGIC
Arthur Weasley, Head of the Misuse of Muggle ArВӯtifacts Office, was today fined fifty Galleons for beВӯwitching a Muggle car.
Mr. Lucius Malfoy, a governor of Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry, where the enchanted car crashed earlier this year, called today for Mr. WeasleyвҖҷs resignation.
вҖңWeasley has brought the Ministry into disreВӯpute,вҖқ Mr. Malfoy told our reporter. вҖңHe is clearly unfit to draw up our laws and his ridiculous MugВӯgle Protection Act should be scrapped immediВӯately.вҖқ
Mr. Weasley was unavailable for comment, alВӯthough his wife told reporters to clear off or sheвҖҷd set the family ghoul on them.
вҖңWell?вҖқ said Malfoy impatiently as Harry handed the clipping back to him. вҖңDonвҖҷt you think itвҖҷs funny?вҖқ
вҖңHa, ha,вҖқ said Harry bleakly.
вҖңArthur Weasley loves Muggles so much he should snap his wand in half and go and join them,вҖқ said Malfoy scornfully. вҖңYouвҖҷd never know the Weasleys were purebloods, the way they behave.вҖқ
RonвҖҷs вҖ” or rather, CrabbeвҖҷs вҖ” face was contorted with fury.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs up with you, Crabbe?вҖқ snapped Malfoy.
вҖңStomachache,вҖқ Ron grunted.
вҖңWell, go up to the hospital wing and give all those Mudbloods a kick from me,вҖқ said Malfoy, snickering. вҖңYou know, IвҖҷm surprised the Daily Prophet hasnвҖҷt reported all these attacks yet,вҖқ he went on thoughtfully. вҖңI suppose DumbledoreвҖҷs trying to hush it all up. HeвҖҷll be sacked if it doesnвҖҷt stop soon. FatherвҖҷs always said old DumbledoreвҖҷs the worst thing thatвҖҷs ever happened to this place. He loves Muggle-borns. A decent headmaster would neverвҖҷve let slime like that Creevey in.вҖқ
Malfoy started taking pictures with an imaginary camera and did a cruel but accurate impression of Colin: вҖң вҖҳPotter, can I have your picture, Potter? Can I have your autograph? Can I lick your shoes, please, Potter?вҖҷ вҖқ
He dropped his hands and looked at Harry and Ron.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs the matter with you two?вҖқ
Far too late, Harry and Ron forced themselves to laugh, but Malfoy seemed satisfied; perhaps Crabbe and Goyle were always slow on the uptake.
вҖңSaint Potter, the MudbloodsвҖҷ friend,вҖқ said Malfoy slowly. вҖңHeвҖҷs another one with no proper wizard feeling, or he wouldnвҖҷt go around with that jumped-up Granger Mudblood. And people think heвҖҷs SlytherinвҖҷs heir!вҖқ
Harry and Ron waited with bated breath: Malfoy was surely secВӯonds away from telling them it was him вҖ” but then вҖ”
вҖңI wish I knew who it is,вҖқ said Malfoy petulantly. вҖңI could help them.вҖқ
RonвҖҷs jaw dropped so that Crabbe looked even more clueless than usual. Fortunately, Malfoy didnвҖҷt notice, and Harry, thinking fast, said, вҖңYou must have some idea whoвҖҷs behind it all. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңYou know I havenвҖҷt, Goyle, how many times do I have to tell you?вҖқ snapped Malfoy. вҖңAnd Father wonвҖҷt tell me anything about the last time the Chamber was opened either. Of course, it was fifty years ago, so it was before his time, but he knows all about it, and he says that it was all kept quiet and itвҖҷll look suspicious if I know too much about it. But I know one thing вҖ” last time the ChamВӯber of Secrets was opened, a Mudblood died. So I bet itвҖҷs a matter of time before one of themвҖҷs killed this time. вҖҰ I hope itвҖҷs Granger,вҖқ he said with relish.
Ron was clenching CrabbeвҖҷs gigantic fists. Feeling that it would be a bit of a giveaway if Ron punched Malfoy, Harry shot him a warning look and said, вҖңDвҖҷyou know if the person who opened the Chamber last time was caught?вҖқ
вҖңOh, yeah вҖҰ whoever it was was expelled,вҖқ said Malfoy. вҖңTheyвҖҷre probably still in Azkaban.вҖқ
вҖңAzkaban?вҖқ said Harry, puzzled.
вҖңAzkaban вҖ” the wizard prison, Goyle,вҖқ said Malfoy, looking at him in disbelief. вҖңHonestly, if you were any slower, youвҖҷd be going backward.вҖқ
He shifted restlessly in his chair and said, вҖңFather says to keep my head down and let the Heir of Slytherin get on with it. He says the school needs ridding of all the Mudblood filth, but not to get mixed up in it. Of course, heвҖҷs got a lot on his plate at the moment. You know the Ministry of Magic raided our manor last week?вҖқ
Harry tried to force GoyleвҖҷs dull face into a look of concern.
вҖңYeah вҖҰвҖқ said Malfoy. вҖңLuckily, they didnвҖҷt find much. FatherвҖҷs got some very valuable Dark Arts stuff. But luckily, weвҖҷve got our own secret chamber under the drawing-room floor вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңHo!вҖқ said Ron.
Malfoy looked at him. So did Harry. Ron blushed. Even his hair was turning red. His nose was also slowly lengthening вҖ” their hour was up, Ron was turning back into himself, and from the look of horror he was suddenly giving Harry, he must be, too.
They both jumped to their feet.
вҖңMedicine for my stomach,вҖқ Ron grunted, and without further ado they sprinted the length of the Slytherin common room, hurled themselves at the stone wall, and dashed up the passage, hoping against hope that Malfoy hadnвҖҷt noticed anything. Harry could feel his feet slipping around in GoyleвҖҷs huge shoes and had to hoist up his robes as he shrank; they crashed up the steps into the dark entrance hall, which was full of a muffled pounding coming from the closet where theyвҖҷd locked Crabbe and Goyle. Leaving their shoes outside the closet door, they sprinted in their socks up the marble staircase toward Moaning MyrtleвҖҷs bathroom.
вҖңWell, it wasnвҖҷt a complete waste of time,вҖқ Ron panted, closing the bathroom door behind them. вҖңI know we still havenвҖҷt found out whoвҖҷs doing the attacks, but IвҖҷm going to write to Dad tomorВӯrow and tell him to check under the MalfoysвҖҷ drawing room.вҖқ
Harry checked his face in the cracked mirror. He was back to normal. He put his glasses on as Ron hammered on the door of HermioneвҖҷs stall.
вҖңHermione, come out, weвҖҷve got loads to tell you вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңGo away!вҖқ Hermione squeaked.
Harry and Ron looked at each other.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs the matter?вҖқ said Ron. вҖңYou must be back to normal by now, we are вҖ”вҖқ
But Moaning Myrtle glided suddenly through the stall door. Harry had never seen her looking so happy.
вҖңOoooooh, wait till you see,вҖқ she said. вҖңItвҖҷs awful вҖ”вҖқ
They heard the lock slide back and Hermione emerged, sobВӯbing, her robes pulled up over her head.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs up?вҖқ said Ron uncertainly. вҖңHave you still got MilliВӯcentвҖҷs nose or something?вҖқ
Hermione let her robes fall and Ron backed into the sink.
Her face was covered in black fur. Her eyes had turned yellow and there were long, pointed ears poking through her hair.
вҖңIt was a c-cat hair!вҖқ she howled. вҖңM-Millicent Bulstrode m-must have a cat! And the p-potion isnвҖҷt supposed to be used for animal transformations!вҖқ
вҖңUh-oh,вҖқ said Ron.
вҖңYouвҖҷll be teased something dreadful,вҖқ said Myrtle happily.
вҖңItвҖҷs okay, Hermione,вҖқ said Harry quickly. вҖңWeвҖҷll take you up to the hospital wing. Madam Pomfrey never asks too many quesВӯtions. вҖҰвҖқ
It took a long time to persuade Hermione to leave the bathВӯroom. Moaning Myrtle sped them on their way with a hearty gufВӯfaw. вҖңWait till everyone finds out youвҖҷve got a tail!вҖқ
## Chapter 13

The Very Secret Diary
Hermione remained in the hospital wing for several weeks. There was a flurry of rumor about her disappearance when the rest of the school arrived back from their Christmas holВӯidays, because of course everyone thought that she had been atВӯtacked. So many students filed past the hospital wing trying to catch a glimpse of her that Madam Pomfrey took out her curtains again and placed them around HermioneвҖҷs bed, to spare her the shame of being seen with a furry face.
Harry and Ron went to visit her every evening. When the new term started, they brought her each dayвҖҷs homework.
вҖңIf IвҖҷd sprouted whiskers, IвҖҷd take a break from work,вҖқ said Ron, tipping a stack of books onto HermioneвҖҷs bedside table one evening.
вҖңDonвҖҷt be silly, Ron, IвҖҷve got to keep up,вҖқ said Hermione briskly. Her spirits were greatly improved by the fact that all the hair had gone from her face and her eyes were turning slowly back to brown. вҖңI donвҖҷt suppose youвҖҷve got any new leads?вҖқ she added in a whisper, so that Madam Pomfrey couldnвҖҷt hear her.
вҖңNothing,вҖқ said Harry gloomily.
вҖңI was so sure it was Malfoy,вҖқ said Ron, for about the hundredth time.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs that?вҖқ asked Harry, pointing to something gold sticking out from under HermioneвҖҷs pillow.
вҖңJust a get well card,вҖқ said Hermione hastily, trying to poke it out of sight, but Ron was too quick for her. He pulled it out, flicked it open, and read aloud:
вҖңTo Miss Granger, wishing you a speedy recovery, from your conВӯcerned teacher, Professor Gilderoy Lockhart, Order of Merlin, Third Class, Honorary Member of the Dark Force Defense League, and five-time winner of Witch WeeklyвҖҷs Most-Charming-Smile Award.вҖқ
Ron looked up at Hermione, disgusted.
вҖңYou sleep with this under your pillow?вҖқ
But Hermione was spared answering by Madam Pomfrey sweepВӯing over with her evening dose of medicine.
вҖңIs Lockhart the smarmiest bloke youвҖҷve ever met, or what?вҖқ Ron said to Harry as they left the infirmary and started up the stairs toward Gryffindor Tower. Snape had given them so much homework, Harry thought he was likely to be in the sixth year beВӯfore he finished it. Ron was just saying he wished he had asked Hermione how many rat tails you were supposed to add to a Hair-Raising Potion when an angry outburst from the floor above reached their ears.
вҖңThatвҖҷs Filch,вҖқ Harry muttered as they hurried up the stairs and paused, out of sight, listening hard.
вҖңYou donвҖҷt think someone elseвҖҷs been attacked?вҖқ said Ron tensely.
They stood still, their heads inclined toward FilchвҖҷs voice, which sounded quite hysterical.
вҖңвҖ” even more work for me! Mopping all night, like I havenвҖҷt got enough to do! No, this is the final straw, IвҖҷm going to Dumbledore вҖ”вҖқ
His footsteps receded along the out-of-sight corridor and they heard a distant door slam.
They poked their heads around the corner. Filch had clearly been manning his usual lookout post: They were once again on the spot where Mrs. Norris had been attacked. They saw at a glance what Filch had been shouting about. A great flood of water stretched over half the corridor, and it looked as though it was still seeping from under the door of Moaning MyrtleвҖҷs bathroom. Now that Filch had stopped shouting, they could hear MyrtleвҖҷs wails echoing off the bathroom walls.
вҖңNow whatвҖҷs up with her?вҖқ said Ron.
вҖңLetвҖҷs go and see,вҖқ said Harry, and holding their robes over their ankles they stepped through the great wash of water to the door bearing its OUT OF ORDER sign, ignored it as always, and entered.
Moaning Myrtle was crying, if possible, louder and harder than ever before. She seemed to be hiding down her usual toilet. It was dark in the bathroom because the candles had been extinguished in the great rush of water that had left both walls and floor soaking wet.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs up, Myrtle?вҖқ said Harry.
вҖңWhoвҖҷs that?вҖқ glugged Myrtle miserably. вҖңCome to throw someВӯthing else at me?вҖқ
Harry waded across to her stall and said, вҖңWhy would I throw something at you?вҖқ
вҖңDonвҖҷt ask me,вҖқ Myrtle shouted, emerging with a wave of yet more water, which splashed onto the already sopping floor. вҖңHere I am, minding my own business, and someone thinks itвҖҷs funny to throw a book at me. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңBut it canвҖҷt hurt you if someone throws something at you,вҖқ said Harry, reasonably. вҖңI mean, itвҖҷd just go right through you, wouldnвҖҷt it?вҖқ
He had said the wrong thing. Myrtle puffed herself up and shrieked, вҖңLetвҖҷs all throw books at Myrtle, because she canвҖҷt feel it! Ten points if you can get it through her stomach! Fifty points if it goes through her head! Well, ha, ha, ha! What a lovely game, I donвҖҷt think!вҖқ
вҖңWho threw it at you, anyway?вҖқ asked Harry.
вҖңI donвҖҷt know. вҖҰ I was just sitting in the U-bend, thinking about death, and it fell right through the top of my head,вҖқ said Myrtle, glaring at them. вҖңItвҖҷs over there, it got washed out. вҖҰвҖқ
Harry and Ron looked under the sink where Myrtle was pointВӯing. A small, thin book lay there. It had a shabby black cover and was as wet as everything else in the bathroom. Harry stepped forВӯward to pick it up, but Ron suddenly flung out an arm to hold him back.
вҖңWhat?вҖқ said Harry.
вҖңAre you crazy?вҖқ said Ron. вҖңIt could be dangerous.вҖқ
вҖңDangerous?вҖқ said Harry, laughing. вҖңCome off it, how could it be dangerous?вҖқ
вҖңYouвҖҷd be surprised,вҖқ said Ron, who was looking apprehensively at the book. вҖңSome of the books the MinistryвҖҷs confiscated вҖ” DadвҖҷs told me вҖ” there was one that burned your eyes out. And everyone who read Sonnets of a Sorcerer spoke in limericks for the rest of their lives. And some old witch in Bath had a book that you could never stop reading! You just had to wander around with your nose in it, trying to do everything one-handed. And вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңAll right, IвҖҷve got the point,вҖқ said Harry.
The little book lay on the floor, nondescript and soggy.
вҖңWell, we wonвҖҷt find out unless we look at it,вҖқ he said, and he ducked around Ron and picked it up off the floor.
Harry saw at once that it was a diary, and the faded year on the cover told him it was fifty years old. He opened it eagerly. On the first page he could just make out the name вҖңT. M. RiddleвҖқ in smudged ink.
вҖңHang on,вҖқ said Ron, who had approached cautiously and was looking over HarryвҖҷs shoulder. вҖңI know that name. вҖҰ T. M. RidВӯdle got an award for special services to the school fifty years ago.вҖқ
вҖңHow on earth dвҖҷyou know that?вҖқ said Harry in amazement.
вҖңBecause Filch made me polish his shield about fifty times in deВӯtention,вҖқ said Ron resentfully. вҖңThat was the one I burped slugs all over. If youвҖҷd wiped slime off a name for an hour, youвҖҷd remember it, too.вҖқ
Harry peeled the wet pages apart. They were completely blank. There wasnвҖҷt the faintest trace of writing on any of them, not even Auntie MabelвҖҷs birthday, or dentist, half-past three.
вҖңHe never wrote in it,вҖқ said Harry, disappointed.
вҖңI wonder why someone wanted to flush it away?вҖқ said Ron cuВӯriously.
Harry turned to the back cover of the book and saw the printed name of a variety store on Vauxhall Road, London.
вҖңHe mustвҖҷve been Muggle-born,вҖқ said Harry thoughtfully. вҖңTo have bought a diary from Vauxhall Road. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңWell, itвҖҷs not much use to you,вҖқ said Ron. He dropped his voice. вҖңFifty points if you can get it through MyrtleвҖҷs nose.вҖқ
Harry, however, pocketed it.
Hermione left the hospital wing, de-whiskered, tail-less, and fur-free, at the beginning of February. On her first evening back in Gryffindor Tower, Harry showed her T. M. RiddleвҖҷs diary and told her the story of how they had found it.
вҖңOooh, it might have hidden powers,вҖқ said Hermione enthusiВӯastically, taking the diary and looking at it closely.
вҖңIf it has, itвҖҷs hiding them very well,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңMaybe itвҖҷs shy. I donвҖҷt know why you donвҖҷt chuck it, Harry.вҖқ
вҖңI wish I knew why someone did try to chuck it,вҖқ said Harry. вҖңI wouldnвҖҷt mind knowing how Riddle got an award for special serВӯvices to Hogwarts either.вҖқ
вҖңCouldвҖҷve been anything,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңMaybe he got thirty O.W.L.s or saved a teacher from the giant squid. Maybe he murВӯdered Myrtle; that wouldвҖҷve done everyone a favor. вҖҰвҖқ
But Harry could tell from the arrested look on HermioneвҖҷs face that she was thinking what he was thinking.
вҖңWhat?вҖқ said Ron, looking from one to the other.
вҖңWell, the Chamber of Secrets was opened fifty years ago, wasnвҖҷt it?вҖқ he said. вҖңThatвҖҷs what Malfoy said.вҖқ
вҖңYeah вҖҰвҖқ said Ron slowly.
вҖңAnd this diary is fifty years old,вҖқ said Hermione, tapping it exВӯcitedly.
вҖңSo?вҖқ
вҖңOh, Ron, wake up,вҖқ snapped Hermione. вҖңWe know the person who opened the Chamber last time was expelled fifty years ago. We know T. M. Riddle got an award for special services to the school fifty years ago. Well, what if Riddle got his special award for catchВӯing the Heir of Slytherin? His diary would probably tell us everyВӯthing вҖ” where the Chamber is, and how to open it, and what sort of creature lives in it вҖ” the person whoвҖҷs behind the attacks this time wouldnвҖҷt want that lying around, would they?вҖқ
вҖңThatвҖҷs a brilliant theory, Hermione,вҖқ said Ron, вҖңwith just one tiny little flaw. ThereвҖҷs nothing written in his diary.вҖқ
But Hermione was pulling her wand out of her bag.
вҖңIt might be invisible ink!вҖқ she whispered.
She tapped the diary three times and said, вҖңAparecium!вҖқ
Nothing happened. Undaunted, Hermione shoved her hand back into her bag and pulled out what appeared to be a bright red eraser.
вҖңItвҖҷs a Revealer, I got it in Diagon Alley,вҖқ she said.
She rubbed hard on January first. Nothing happened.
вҖңIвҖҷm telling you, thereвҖҷs nothing to find in there,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңRiddle just got a diary for Christmas and couldnвҖҷt be bothered filling it in.вҖқ
Harry couldnвҖҷt explain, even to himself, why he didnвҖҷt just throw RiddleвҖҷs diary away. The fact was that even though he knew the diВӯary was blank, he kept absentmindedly picking it up and turnВӯing the pages, as though it were a story he wanted to finish. And while Harry was sure he had never heard the name T. M. Riddle before, it still seemed to mean something to him, almost as though Riddle was a friend heвҖҷd had when he was very small, and had half-forgotten. But this was absurd. HeвҖҷd never had friends before Hogwarts, Dudley had made sure of that.
Nevertheless, Harry was determined to find out more about Riddle, so next day at break, he headed for the trophy room to exВӯamine RiddleвҖҷs special award, accompanied by an interested HerВӯmione and a thoroughly unconvinced Ron, who told them heвҖҷd seen enough of the trophy room to last him a lifetime.
RiddleвҖҷs burnished gold shield was tucked away in a corner cabВӯinet. It didnвҖҷt carry details of why it had been given to him (вҖңGood thing, too, or itвҖҷd be even bigger and IвҖҷd still be polishing it,вҖқ said Ron). However, they did find RiddleвҖҷs name on an old Medal for Magical Merit, and on a list of old Head Boys.
вҖңHe sounds like Percy,вҖқ said Ron, wrinkling his nose in disgust. вҖңPrefect, Head Boy вҖҰ probably top of every class вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңYou say that like itвҖҷs a bad thing,вҖқ said Hermione in a slightly hurt voice.
The sun had now begun to shine weakly on Hogwarts again. Inside the castle, the mood had grown more hopeful. There had been no more attacks since those on Justin and Nearly Headless Nick, and Madam Pomfrey was pleased to report that the Mandrakes were becoming moody and secretive, meaning that they were fast leavВӯing childhood.
вҖңThe moment their acne clears up, theyвҖҷll be ready for repotting again,вҖқ Harry heard her telling Filch kindly one afternoon. вҖңAnd after that, it wonвҖҷt be long until weвҖҷre cutting them up and stewing them. YouвҖҷll have Mrs. Norris back in no time.вҖқ
Perhaps the Heir of Slytherin had lost his or her nerve, thought Harry. It must be getting riskier and riskier to open the Chamber of Secrets, with the school so alert and suspicious. Perhaps the monster, whatever it was, was even now settling itself down to hiВӯbernate for another fifty years. вҖҰ
Ernie Macmillan of Hufflepuff didnвҖҷt take this cheerful view. He was still convinced that Harry was the guilty one, that he had вҖңgiven himself awayвҖқ at the Dueling Club. Peeves wasnвҖҷt helping matters; he kept popping up in the crowded corridors singing вҖңOh, Potter, you rotter вҖҰвҖқ now with a dance routine to match.
Gilderoy Lockhart seemed to think he himself had made the atВӯtacks stop. Harry overheard him telling Professor McGonagall so while the Gryffindors were lining up for Transfiguration.
вҖңI donвҖҷt think thereвҖҷll be any more trouble, Minerva,вҖқ he said, tapping his nose knowingly and winking. вҖңI think the Chamber has been locked for good this time. The culprit must have known it was only a matter of time before I caught him. Rather sensible to stop now, before I came down hard on him.
вҖңYou know, what the school needs now is a morale-booster. Wash away the memories of last term! I wonвҖҷt say any more just now, but I think I know just the thing. вҖҰвҖқ
He tapped his nose again and strode off.
LockhartвҖҷs idea of a morale-booster became clear at breakfast time on February fourteenth. Harry hadnвҖҷt had much sleep because of a late-running Quidditch practice the night before, and he hurВӯried down to the Great Hall, slightly late. He thought, for a moВӯment, that heвҖҷd walked through the wrong doors.
The walls were all covered with large, lurid pink flowers. Worse still, heart-shaped confetti was falling from the pale blue ceiling. Harry went over to the Gryffindor table, where Ron was sitting looking sickened, and Hermione seemed to have been overcome with giggles.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs going on?вҖқ Harry asked them, sitting down and wiping confetti off his bacon.
Ron pointed to the teachersвҖҷ table, apparently too disgusted to speak. Lockhart, wearing lurid pink robes to match the decoraВӯtions, was waving for silence. The teachers on either side of him were looking stony-faced. From where he sat, Harry could see a muscle going in Professor McGonagallвҖҷs cheek. Snape looked as though someone had just fed him a large beaker of Skele-Gro.
вҖңHappy ValentineвҖҷs Day!вҖқ Lockhart shouted. вҖңAnd may I thank the forty-six people who have so far sent me cards! Yes, I have taken the liberty of arranging this little surprise for you all вҖ” and it doesnвҖҷt end here!вҖқ
Lockhart clapped his hands and through the doors to the entrance hall marched a dozen surly-looking dwarfs. Not just any dwarfs, however. Lockhart had them all wearing golden wings and carrying harps.
вҖңMy friendly, card-carrying cupids!вҖқ beamed Lockhart. вҖңThey will be roving around the school today delivering your valentines! And the fun doesnвҖҷt stop here! IвҖҷm sure my colleagues will want to enter into the spirit of the occasion! Why not ask Professor Snape to show you how to whip up a Love Potion! And while youвҖҷre at it, Professor Flitwick knows more about Entrancing Enchantments than any wizard IвҖҷve ever met, the sly old dog!вҖқ
Professor Flitwick buried his face in his hands. Snape was looking as though the first person to ask him for a Love Potion would be force-fed poison.
вҖңPlease, Hermione, tell me you werenвҖҷt one of the forty-six,вҖқ said Ron as they left the Great Hall for their first lesson. Hermione sudВӯdenly became very interested in searching her bag for her schedule and didnвҖҷt answer.
All day long, the dwarfs kept barging into their classes to deliver valentines, to the annoyance of the teachers, and late that afterВӯnoon as the Gryffindors were walking upstairs for Charms, one of the dwarfs caught up with Harry.
вҖңOy, you! вҖҷArry Potter!вҖқ shouted a particularly grim-looking dwarf, elbowing people out of the way to get to Harry.
Hot all over at the thought of being given a valentine in front of a line of first years, which happened to include Ginny Weasley, Harry tried to escape. The dwarf, however, cut his way through the crowd by kicking peopleвҖҷs shins, and reached him before heвҖҷd gone two paces.
вҖңIвҖҷve got a musical message to deliver to вҖҷArry Potter in person,вҖқ he said, twanging his harp in a threatening sort of way.
вҖңNot here,вҖқ Harry hissed, trying to escape.
вҖңStay still!вҖқ grunted the dwarf, grabbing hold of HarryвҖҷs bag and pulling him back.
вҖңLet me go!вҖқ Harry snarled, tugging.
With a loud ripping noise, his bag split in two. His books, wand, parchment, and quill spilled onto the floor and his ink bottle smashed over everything.
Harry scrambled around, trying to pick it all up before the dwarf started singing, causing something of a holdup in the corridor.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs going on here?вҖқ came the cold, drawling voice of Draco Malfoy. Harry started stuffing everything feverishly into his ripped bag, desperate to get away before Malfoy could hear his musical valentine.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs all this commotion?вҖқ said another familiar voice as Percy Weasley arrived.
Losing his head, Harry tried to make a run for it, but the dwarf seized him around the knees and brought him crashing to the floor.
вҖңRight,вҖқ he said, sitting on HarryвҖҷs ankles. вҖңHere is your singing valentine:
His eyes are as green as a fresh pickled toad,
His hair is as dark as a blackboard.
I wish he was mine, heвҖҷs really divine,
The hero who conquered the Dark Lord.вҖқ
Harry would have given all the gold in Gringotts to evaporate on the spot. Trying valiantly to laugh along with everyone else, he got up, his feet numb from the weight of the dwarf, as Percy Weasley did his best to disperse the crowd, some of whom were crying with mirth.
вҖңOff you go, off you go, the bell rang five minutes ago, off to class, now,вҖқ he said, shooing some of the younger students away. вҖңAnd you, Malfoy вҖ”вҖқ
Harry, glancing over, saw Malfoy stoop and snatch up someВӯthing. Leering, he showed it to Crabbe and Goyle, and Harry realВӯized that heвҖҷd got RiddleвҖҷs diary.
вҖңGive that back,вҖқ said Harry quietly.
вҖңWonder what PotterвҖҷs written in this?вҖқ said Malfoy, who obviously hadnвҖҷt noticed the year on the cover and thought he had HarryвҖҷs own diary. A hush fell over the onlookers. Ginny was starВӯing from the diary to Harry, looking terrified.
вҖңHand it over, Malfoy,вҖқ said Percy sternly.
вҖңWhen IвҖҷve had a look,вҖқ said Malfoy, waving the diary tauntВӯingly at Harry.
Percy said, вҖңAs a school prefect вҖ”вҖқ but Harry had lost his temВӯper. He pulled out his wand and shouted, вҖңExpelliarmus!вҖқ and just as Snape had disarmed Lockhart, so Malfoy found the diary shootВӯing out of his hand into the air. Ron, grinning broadly, caught it.
вҖңHarry!вҖқ said Percy loudly. вҖңNo magic in the corridors. IвҖҷll have to report this, you know!вҖқ
But Harry didnвҖҷt care, he was one-up on Malfoy, and that was worth five points from Gryffindor any day. Malfoy was looking fuВӯrious, and as Ginny passed him to enter her classroom, he yelled spitefully after her, вҖңI donвҖҷt think Potter liked your valentine much!вҖқ
Ginny covered her face with her hands and ran into class. Snarling, Ron pulled out his wand, too, but Harry pulled him away. Ron didnвҖҷt need to spend the whole of Charms belching slugs.
It wasnвҖҷt until they had reached Professor FlitwickвҖҷs class that Harry noticed something rather odd about RiddleвҖҷs diary. All his other books were drenched in scarlet ink. The diary, however, was as clean as it had been before the ink bottle had smashed all over it. He tried to point this out to Ron, but Ron was having trouble with his wand again; large purple bubbles were blossoming out of the end, and he wasnвҖҷt much interested in anything else.
* * *
Harry went to bed before anyone else in his dormitory that night. This was partly because he didnвҖҷt think he could stand Fred and George singing, вҖңHis eyes are as green as a fresh pickled toadвҖқ one more time, and partly because he wanted to examine RiddleвҖҷs diary again, and knew that Ron thought he was wasting his time.
Harry sat on his four-poster and flicked through the blank pages, not one of which had a trace of scarlet ink on it. Then he pulled a new bottle out of his bedside cabinet, dipped his quill into it, and dropped a blot onto the first page of the diary.
The ink shone brightly on the paper for a second and then, as though it was being sucked into the page, vanished. Excited, Harry loaded up his quill a second time and wrote, вҖңMy name is Harry Potter.вҖқ
The words shone momentarily on the page and they, too, sank without trace. Then, at last, something happened.
Oozing back out of the page, in his very own ink, came words Harry had never written.
вҖңHello, Harry Potter. My name is Tom Riddle. How did you come by my diary?вҖқ
These words, too, faded away, but not before Harry had started to scribble back.
вҖңSomeone tried to flush it down a toilet.вҖқ
He waited eagerly for RiddleвҖҷs reply.
вҖңLucky that I recorded my memories in some more lasting way than ink. But I always knew that there would be those who would not want this diary read.вҖқ
вҖңWhat do you mean?вҖқ Harry scrawled, blotting the page in his excitement.
вҖңI mean that this diary holds memories of terrible things. Things that were covered up. Things that happened at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry.вҖқ
вҖңThatвҖҷs where I am now,вҖқ Harry wrote quickly. вҖңIвҖҷm at HogВӯwarts, and horrible stuffвҖҷs been happening. Do you know anything about the Chamber of Secrets?вҖқ
His heart was hammering. RiddleвҖҷs reply came quickly, his writВӯing becoming untidier, as though he was hurrying to tell all he knew.
вҖңOf course I know about the Chamber of Secrets. In my day, they told us it was a legend, that it did not exist. But this was a lie. In my fifth year, the Chamber was opened and the monster attacked several students, finally killing one. I caught the person whoвҖҷd opened the Chamber and he was expelled. But the headmaster, Professor Dippet, ashamed that such a thing had happened at Hogwarts, forbade me to tell the truth. A story was given out that the girl had died in a freak acВӯcident. They gave me a nice, shiny, engraved trophy for my trouble and warned me to keep my mouth shut. But I knew it could happen again. The monster lived on, and the one who had the power to release it was not imprisoned.вҖқ
Harry nearly upset his ink bottle in his hurry to write back.
вҖңItвҖҷs happening again now. There have been three attacks and no one seems to know whoвҖҷs behind them. Who was it last time?вҖқ
вҖңI can show you, if you like,вҖқ came RiddleвҖҷs reply. вҖңYou donвҖҷt have to take my word for it. I can take you inside my memory of the night when I caught him.вҖқ
Harry hesitated, his quill suspended over the diary. What did Riddle mean? How could he be taken inside somebody elseвҖҷs memВӯory? He glanced nervously at the door to the dormitory, which was growing dark. When he looked back at the diary, he saw fresh words forming.
вҖңLet me show you.вҖқ
Harry paused for a fraction of a second and then wrote two letters.
вҖңOK.вҖқ
The pages of the diary began to blow as though caught in a high wind, stopping halfway through the month of June. Mouth hangВӯing open, Harry saw that the little square for June thirteenth seemed to have turned into a minuscule television screen. His hands trembling slightly, he raised the book to press his eye against the little window, and before he knew what was happening, he was tilting forward; the window was widening, he felt his body leave his bed, and he was pitched headfirst through the opening in the page, into a whirl of color and shadow.
He felt his feet hit solid ground, and stood, shaking, as the blurred shapes around him came suddenly into focus.
He knew immediately where he was. This circular room with the sleeping portraits was DumbledoreвҖҷs office вҖ” but it wasnвҖҷt Dumbledore who was sitting behind the desk. A wizened, frail-looking wizard, bald except for a few wisps of white hair, was readВӯing a letter by candlelight. Harry had never seen this man before.
вҖңIвҖҷm sorry,вҖқ he said shakily. вҖңI didnвҖҷt mean to butt in вҖ”вҖқ
But the wizard didnвҖҷt look up. He continued to read, frowning slightly. Harry drew nearer to his desk and stammered, вҖңEr вҖ” IвҖҷll just go, shall I?вҖқ
Still the wizard ignored him. He didnвҖҷt seem even to have heard him. Thinking that the wizard might be deaf, Harry raised his voice.
вҖңSorry I disturbed you. IвҖҷll go now,вҖқ he half-shouted.
The wizard folded up the letter with a sigh, stood up, walked past Harry without glancing at him, and went to draw the curtains at his window.
The sky outside the window was ruby-red; it seemed to be sunВӯset. The wizard went back to the desk, sat down, and twiddled his thumbs, watching the door.
Harry looked around the office. No Fawkes the phoenix вҖ” no whirring silver contraptions. This was Hogwarts as Riddle had known it, meaning that this unknown wizard was headmaster, not Dumbledore, and he, Harry, was little more than a phantom, comВӯpletely invisible to the people of fifty years ago.
There was a knock on the office door.
вҖңEnter,вҖқ said the old wizard in a feeble voice.
A boy of about sixteen entered, taking off his pointed hat. A silВӯver prefectвҖҷs badge was glinting on his chest. He was much taller than Harry, but he, too, had jet-black hair.
вҖңAh, Riddle,вҖқ said the headmaster.
вҖңYou wanted to see me, Professor Dippet?вҖқ said Riddle. He looked nervous.
вҖңSit down,вҖқ said Dippet. вҖңIвҖҷve just been reading the letter you sent me.вҖқ
вҖңOh,вҖқ said Riddle. He sat down, gripping his hands together very tightly.
вҖңMy dear boy,вҖқ said Dippet kindly, вҖңI cannot possibly let you stay at school over the summer. Surely you want to go home for the holidays?вҖқ
вҖңNo,вҖқ said Riddle at once. вҖңIвҖҷd much rather stay at Hogwarts than go back to that вҖ” to that вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңYou live in a Muggle orphanage during the holidays, I believe?вҖқ said Dippet curiously.
вҖңYes, sir,вҖқ said Riddle, reddening slightly.
вҖңYou are Muggle-born?вҖқ
вҖңHalf-blood, sir,вҖқ said Riddle. вҖңMuggle father, witch mother.вҖқ
вҖңAnd are both your parents вҖ” ?вҖқ
вҖңMy mother died just after I was born, sir. They told me at the orphanage she lived just long enough to name me вҖ” Tom after my father, Marvolo after my grandfather.вҖқ
Dippet clucked his tongue sympathetically.
вҖңThe thing is, Tom,вҖқ he sighed, вҖңspecial arrangements might have been made for you, but in the current circumstances. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңYou mean all these attacks, sir?вҖқ said Riddle, and HarryвҖҷs heart leapt, and he moved closer, scared of missing anything.
вҖңPrecisely,вҖқ said the headmaster. вҖңMy dear boy, you must see how foolish it would be of me to allow you to remain at the castle when term ends. Particularly in light of the recent tragedy вҖҰ the death of that poor little girl. вҖҰ You will be safer by far at your orВӯphanage. As a matter of fact, the Ministry of Magic is even now talking about closing the school. We are no nearer locating the вҖ” er вҖ” source of all this unpleasantness. вҖҰвҖқ
RiddleвҖҷs eyes had widened.
вҖңSir вҖ” if the person was caught вҖ” if it all stopped вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңWhat do you mean?вҖқ said Dippet with a squeak in his voice, sitting up in his chair. вҖңRiddle, do you mean you know something about these attacks?вҖқ
вҖңNo, sir,вҖқ said Riddle quickly.
But Harry was sure it was the same sort of вҖңnoвҖқ that he himself had given Dumbledore.
Dippet sank back, looking faintly disappointed.
вҖңYou may go, Tom. вҖҰвҖқ
Riddle slid off his chair and slouched out of the room. Harry folВӯlowed him.
Down the moving spiral staircase they went, emerging next to the gargoyle in the darkening corridor. Riddle stopped, and so did Harry, watching him. Harry could tell that Riddle was doing some serious thinking. He was biting his lip, his forehead furВӯrowed.
Then, as though he had suddenly reached a decision, he hurried off, Harry gliding noiselessly behind him. They didnвҖҷt see another person until they reached the entrance hall, when a tall wizard with long, sweeping auburn hair and a beard called to Riddle from the marble staircase.
вҖңWhat are you doing, wandering around this late, Tom?вҖқ
Harry gaped at the wizard. He was none other than a fifty-year-younger Dumbledore.
вҖңI had to see the headmaster, sir,вҖқ said Riddle.
вҖңWell, hurry off to bed,вҖқ said Dumbledore, giving Riddle exВӯactly the kind of penetrating stare Harry knew so well. вҖңBest not to roam the corridors these days. Not since вҖҰвҖқ
He sighed heavily, bade Riddle good night, and strode off. RidВӯdle watched him walk out of sight and then, moving quickly, headed straight down the stone steps to the dungeons, with Harry in hot pursuit.
But to HarryвҖҷs disappointment, Riddle led him not into a hidВӯden passageway or a secret tunnel but to the very dungeon in which Harry had Potions with Snape. The torches hadnвҖҷt been lit, and when Riddle pushed the door almost closed, Harry could only just see him, standing stock-still by the door, watching the passage outВӯside.
It felt to Harry that they were there for at least an hour. All he could see was the figure of Riddle at the door, staring through the crack, waiting like a statue. And just when Harry had stopped feelВӯing expectant and tense and started wishing he could return to the present, he heard something move beyond the door.
Someone was creeping along the passage. He heard whoever it was pass the dungeon where he and Riddle were hidden. Riddle, quiet as a shadow, edged through the door and followed, Harry tipВӯtoeing behind him, forgetting that he couldnвҖҷt be heard.
For perhaps five minutes they followed the footsteps, until RidВӯdle stopped suddenly, his head inclined in the direction of new noises. Harry heard a door creak open, and then someone speaking in a hoarse whisper.
вҖңCвҖҷmon вҖҰ gotta get yeh outta here. вҖҰ CвҖҷmon now вҖҰ in the box вҖҰвҖқ
There was something familiar about that voice. вҖҰ
Riddle suddenly jumped around the corner. Harry stepped out behind him. He could see the dark outline of a huge boy who was crouching in front of an open door, a very large box next to it.
вҖң вҖҷEvening, Rubeus,вҖқ said Riddle sharply.
The boy slammed the door shut and stood up.
вҖңWhat yer doinвҖҷ down here, Tom?вҖқ
Riddle stepped closer.
вҖңItвҖҷs all over,вҖқ he said. вҖңIвҖҷm going to have to turn you in, Rubeus. TheyвҖҷre talking about closing Hogwarts if the attacks donвҖҷt stop.вҖқ
вҖңWhat dвҖҷyeh вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңI donвҖҷt think you meant to kill anyone. But monsters donвҖҷt make good pets. I suppose you just let it out for exercise and вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңIt never killed no one!вҖқ said the large boy, backing against the closed door. From behind him, Harry could hear a funny rustling and clicking.
вҖңCome on, Rubeus,вҖқ said Riddle, moving yet closer. вҖңThe dead girlвҖҷs parents will be here tomorrow. The least Hogwarts can do is make sure that the thing that killed their daughter is slaughВӯtered. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңIt wasnвҖҷt him!вҖқ roared the boy, his voice echoing in the dark passage. вҖңHe wouldnвҖҷ! He never!вҖқ
вҖңStand aside,вҖқ said Riddle, drawing out his wand.
His spell lit the corridor with a sudden flaming light. The door behind the large boy flew open with such force it knocked him into the wall opposite. And out of it came something that made Harry let out a long, piercing scream unheard by anyone вҖ”
A vast, low-slung, hairy body and a tangle of black legs; a gleam of many eyes and a pair of razor-sharp pincers вҖ” Riddle raised his wand again, but he was too late. The thing bowled him over as it scuttled away, tearing up the corridor and out of sight. Riddle scrambled to his feet, looking after it; he raised his wand, but the huge boy leapt on him, seized his wand, and threw him back down, yelling, вҖңNOOOOOOO!вҖқ
The scene whirled, the darkness became complete; Harry felt himself falling and, with a crash, he landed spread-eagled on his four-poster in the Gryffindor dormitory, RiddleвҖҷs diary lying open on his stomach.
Before he had had time to regain his breath, the dormitory door opened and Ron came in.
вҖңThere you are,вҖқ he said.
Harry sat up. He was sweating and shaking.
вҖңWhatвҖҷs up?вҖқ said Ron, looking at him with concern.
вҖңIt was Hagrid, Ron. Hagrid opened the Chamber of Secrets fifty years ago.вҖқ
## Chapter 14

Cornelius Fudge
Harry, Ron, and Hermione had always known that Hagrid had an unfortunate liking for large and monstrous creaВӯtures. During their first year at Hogwarts he had tried to raise a dragon in his little wooden house, and it would be a long time before they forgot the giant, three-headed dog heвҖҷd christened вҖңFluffy.вҖқ And if, as a boy, Hagrid had heard that a monster was hidВӯden somewhere in the castle, Harry was sure heвҖҷd have gone to any lengths for a glimpse of it. HeвҖҷd probably thought it was a shame that the monster had been cooped up so long, and thought it deВӯserved the chance to stretch its many legs; Harry could just imagВӯine the thirteen-year-old Hagrid trying to fit a leash and collar on it. But he was equally certain that Hagrid would never have meant to kill anybody.
Harry half wished he hadnвҖҷt found out how to work RiddleвҖҷs diВӯary. Again and again Ron and Hermione made him recount what heвҖҷd seen, until he was heartily sick of telling them and sick of the long, circular conversations that followed.
вҖңRiddle might have got the wrong person,вҖқ said Hermione. вҖңMaybe it was some other monster that was attacking people. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңHow many monsters dвҖҷyou think this place can hold?вҖқ Ron asked dully.
вҖңWe always knew Hagrid had been expelled,вҖқ said Harry miserВӯably. вҖңAnd the attacks mustвҖҷve stopped after Hagrid was kicked out. Otherwise, Riddle wouldnвҖҷt have got his award.вҖқ
Ron tried a different tack.
вҖңRiddle does sound like Percy вҖ” who asked him to squeal on Hagrid, anyway?вҖқ
вҖңBut the monster had killed someone, Ron,вҖқ said Hermione.
вҖңAnd Riddle was going to go back to some Muggle orphanage if they closed Hogwarts,вҖқ said Harry. вҖңI donвҖҷt blame him for wanting to stay here. вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңYou met Hagrid down Knockturn Alley, didnвҖҷt you, Harry?вҖқ
вҖңHe was buying a Flesh-Eating Slug Repellent,вҖқ said Harry quickly.
The three of them fell silent. After a long pause, Hermione voiced the knottiest question of all in a hesitant voice.
вҖңDo you think we should go and ask Hagrid about it all?вҖқ
вҖңThatвҖҷd be a cheerful visit,вҖқ said Ron. вҖң вҖҳHello, Hagrid. Tell us, have you been setting anything mad and hairy loose in the castle lately?вҖҷ вҖқ
In the end, they decided that they would not say anything to Hagrid unless there was another attack, and as more and more days went by with no whisper from the disembodied voice, they became hopeful that they would never need to talk to him about why he had been expelled. It was now nearly four months since Justin and Nearly Headless Nick had been Petrified, and nearly everybody seemed to think that the attacker, whoever it was, had retired for good. Peeves had finally got bored of his вҖңOh, Potter, you rotterвҖқ song, Ernie Macmillan asked Harry quite politely to pass a bucket of leaping toadstools in Herbology one day, and in March several of the Mandrakes threw a loud and raucous party in greenhouse three. This made Professor Sprout very happy.
вҖңThe moment they start trying to move into each otherвҖҷs pots, weвҖҷll know theyвҖҷre fully mature,вҖқ she told Harry. вҖңThen weвҖҷll be able to revive those poor people in the hospital wing.вҖқ
The second years were given something new to think about during their Easter holidays. The time had come to choose their subjects for the third year, a matter that Hermione, at least, took very seriВӯously.
вҖңIt could affect our whole future,вҖқ she told Harry and Ron as they pored over lists of new subjects, marking them with checks.
вҖңI just want to give up Potions,вҖқ said Harry.
вҖңWe canвҖҷt,вҖқ said Ron gloomily. вҖңWe keep all our old subjects, or IвҖҷdвҖҷve ditched Defense Against the Dark Arts.вҖқ
вҖңBut thatвҖҷs very important!вҖқ said Hermione, shocked.
вҖңNot the way Lockhart teaches it,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңI havenвҖҷt learned anything from him except not to set pixies loose.вҖқ
Neville Longbottom had been sent letters from all the witches and wizards in his family, all giving him different advice on what to choose. Confused and worried, he sat reading the subject lists with his tongue poking out, asking people whether they thought ArithВӯmancy sounded more difficult than the study of Ancient Runes. Dean Thomas, who, like Harry, had grown up with Muggles, ended up closing his eyes and jabbing his wand at the list, then picking the subjects it landed on. Hermione took nobodyвҖҷs advice but signed up for everything.
Harry smiled grimly to himself at the thought of what Uncle Vernon and Aunt Petunia would say if he tried to discuss his career in wizardry with them. Not that he didnвҖҷt get any guidance: Percy Weasley was eager to share his experience.
вҖңDepends where you want to go, Harry,вҖқ he said. вҖңItвҖҷs never too early to think about the future, so IвҖҷd recommend Divination. PeoВӯple say Muggle Studies is a soft option, but I personally think wizВӯards should have a thorough understanding of the non-magical community, particularly if theyвҖҷre thinking of working in close contact with them вҖ” look at my father, he has to deal with MugВӯgle business all the time. My brother Charlie was always more of an outdoor type, so he went for Care of Magical Creatures. Play to your strengths, Harry.вҖқ
But the only thing Harry felt he was really good at was QuidВӯditch. In the end, he chose the same new subjects as Ron, feeling that if he was lousy at them, at least heвҖҷd have someone friendly to help him.
GryffindorвҖҷs next Quidditch match would be against Hufflepuff. Wood was insisting on team practices every night after dinner, so that Harry barely had time for anything but Quidditch and homeВӯwork. However, the training sessions were getting better, or at least drier, and the evening before SaturdayвҖҷs match he went up to his dormitory to drop off his broomstick feeling GryffindorвҖҷs chances for the Quidditch Cup had never been better.
But his cheerful mood didnвҖҷt last long. At the top of the stairs to the dormitory, he met Neville Longbottom, who was looking frantic.
вҖңHarry вҖ” I donвҖҷt know who did it вҖ” I just found вҖ”вҖқ
Watching Harry fearfully, Neville pushed open the door.
The contents of HarryвҖҷs trunk had been thrown everywhere. His cloak lay ripped on the floor. The bedclothes had been pulled off his four-poster and the drawer had been pulled out of his bedside cabinet, the contents strewn over the mattress.
Harry walked over to the bed, openmouthed, treading on a few loose pages of Travels with Trolls. As he and Neville pulled the blanВӯkets back onto his bed, Ron, Dean, and Seamus came in. Dean swore loudly.
вҖңWhat happened, Harry?вҖқ
вҖңNo idea,вҖқ said Harry. But Ron was examining HarryвҖҷs robes. All the pockets were hanging out.
вҖңSomeoneвҖҷs been looking for something,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңIs there anything missing?вҖқ
Harry started to pick up all his things and throw them into his trunk. It was only as he threw the last of the Lockhart books back into it that he realized what wasnвҖҷt there.
вҖңRiddleвҖҷs diaryвҖҷs gone,вҖқ he said in an undertone to Ron.
вҖңWhat?вҖқ
Harry jerked his head toward the dormitory door and Ron folВӯlowed him out. They hurried down to the Gryffindor common room, which was half-empty, and joined Hermione, who was sitВӯting alone, reading a book called Ancient Runes Made Easy.
Hermione looked aghast at the news.
вҖңBut вҖ” only a Gryffindor could have stolen вҖ” nobody else knows our password вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңExactly,вҖқ said Harry.
They woke the next day to brilliant sunshine and a light, refreshing breeze.
вҖңPerfect Quidditch conditions!вҖқ said Wood enthusiastically at the Gryffindor table, loading the teamвҖҷs plates with scrambled eggs. вҖңHarry, buck up there, you need a decent breakfast.вҖқ
Harry had been staring down the packed Gryffindor table, wonВӯdering if the new owner of RiddleвҖҷs diary was right in front of his eyes. Hermione had been urging him to report the robbery, but Harry didnвҖҷt like the idea. HeвҖҷd have to tell a teacher all about the diary, and how many people knew why Hagrid had been expelled fifty years ago? He didnвҖҷt want to be the one who brought it all up again.
As he left the Great Hall with Ron and Hermione to go and colВӯlect his Quidditch things, another very serious worry was added to HarryвҖҷs growing list. He had just set foot on the marble staircase when he heard it yet again вҖ”
вҖңKill this time вҖҰ let me rip вҖҰ tear вҖҰвҖқ
He shouted aloud and Ron and Hermione both jumped away from him in alarm.
вҖңThe voice!вҖқ said Harry, looking over his shoulder. вҖңI just heard it again вҖ” didnвҖҷt you?вҖқ
Ron shook his head, wide-eyed. Hermione, however, clapped a hand to her forehead.
вҖңHarry вҖ” I think IвҖҷve just understood something! IвҖҷve got to go to the library!вҖқ
And she sprinted away, up the stairs.
вҖңWhat does she understand?вҖқ said Harry distractedly, still lookВӯing around, trying to tell where the voice had come from.
вҖңLoads more than I do,вҖқ said Ron, shaking his head.
вҖңBut whyвҖҷs she got to go to the library?вҖқ
вҖңBecause thatвҖҷs what Hermione does,вҖқ said Ron, shrugging. вҖңWhen in doubt, go to the library.вҖқ
Harry stood, irresolute, trying to catch the voice again, but people were now emerging from the Great Hall behind him, talkВӯing loudly, exiting through the front doors on their way to the Quidditch pitch.
вҖңYouвҖҷd better get moving,вҖқ said Ron. вҖңItвҖҷs nearly eleven вҖ” the match вҖ”вҖқ
Harry raced up to Gryffindor Tower, collected his Nimbus Two Thousand, and joined the large crowd swarming across the grounds, but his mind was still in the castle along with the bodiless voice, and as he pulled on his scarlet robes in the locker room, his only comfort was that everyone was now outside to watch the game.
The teams walked onto the field to tumultuous applause. Oliver Wood took off for a warm-up flight around the goal posts; Madam Hooch released the balls. The Hufflepuffs, who played in canary yellow, were standing in a huddle, having a last-minute discussion of tactics.
Harry was just mounting his broom when Professor McGonaВӯgall came half marching, half running across the pitch, carrying an enormous purple megaphone.
HarryвҖҷs heart dropped like a stone.
вҖңThis match has been canceled,вҖқ Professor McGonagall called through the megaphone, addressing the packed stadium. There were boos and shouts. Oliver Wood, looking devastated, landed and ran toward Professor McGonagall without getting off his broomstick.
вҖңBut, Professor!вҖқ he shouted. вҖңWeвҖҷve got to play вҖ” the Cup вҖ” Gryffindor вҖ”вҖқ
Professor McGonagall ignored him and continued to shout through her megaphone:
вҖңAll students are to make their way back to the House common rooms, where their Heads of Houses will give them further inforВӯmation. As quickly as you can, please!вҖқ
Then she lowered the megaphone and beckoned Harry over to her.
вҖңPotter, I think youвҖҷd better come with me. вҖҰвҖқ
Wondering how she could possibly suspect him this time, Harry saw Ron detach himself from the complaining crowd; he came running up to them as they set off toward the castle. To HarryвҖҷs surВӯprise, Professor McGonagall didnвҖҷt object.
вҖңYes, perhaps youвҖҷd better come, too, Weasley. вҖҰвҖқ
Some of the students swarming around them were grumbling about the match being canceled; others looked worried. Harry and Ron followed Professor McGonagall back into the school and up the marble staircase. But they werenвҖҷt taken to anybodyвҖҷs office this time.
вҖңThis will be a bit of a shock,вҖқ said Professor McGonagall in a surprisingly gentle voice as they approached the infirmary. вҖңThere has been another attack вҖҰ another double attack.вҖқ
HarryвҖҷs insides did a horrible somersault. Professor McGonagall pushed the door open and he and Ron entered.
Madam Pomfrey was bending over a sixth-year girl with long, curly hair. Harry recognized her as the Ravenclaw theyвҖҷd accidenВӯtally asked for directions to the Slytherin common room. And on the bed next to her was вҖ”
вҖңHermione!вҖқ Ron groaned.
Hermione lay utterly still, her eyes open and glassy.
вҖңThey were found near the library,вҖқ said Professor McGonagall. вҖңI donвҖҷt suppose either of you can explain this? It was on the floor next to them. вҖҰвҖқ
She was holding up a small, circular mirror.
Harry and Ron shook their heads, both staring at Hermione.
вҖңI will escort you back to Gryffindor Tower,вҖқ said ProfesВӯsor McGonagall heavily. вҖңI need to address the students in any case.вҖқ
вҖңAll students will return to their House common rooms by six oвҖҷclock in the evening. No student is to leave the dormitories after that time. You will be escorted to each lesson by a teacher. No stuВӯdent is to use the bathroom unaccompanied by a teacher. All furВӯther Quidditch training and matches are to be postponed. There will be no more evening activities.вҖқ
The Gryffindors packed inside the common room listened to Professor McGonagall in silence. She rolled up the parchment from which she had been reading and said in a somewhat choked voice, вҖңI need hardly add that I have rarely been so distressed. It is likely that the school will be closed unless the culprit behind these attacks is caught. I would urge anyone who thinks they might know anything about them to come forward.вҖқ
She climbed somewhat awkwardly out of the portrait hole, and the Gryffindors began talking immediately.
вҖңThatвҖҷs two Gryffindors down, not counting a Gryffindor ghost, one Ravenclaw, and one Hufflepuff,вҖқ said the Weasley twinsвҖҷ friend Lee Jordan, counting on his fingers. вҖңHavenвҖҷt any of the teachers noticed that the Slytherins are all safe? IsnвҖҷt it obvious all this stuffвҖҷs coming from Slytherin? The Heir of Slytherin, the monster of Slytherin вҖ” why donвҖҷt they just chuck all the Slytherins out?вҖқ he roared, to nods and scattered applause.
Percy Weasley was sitting in a chair behind Lee, but for once he didnвҖҷt seem keen to make his views heard. He was looking pale and stunned.
вҖңPercyвҖҷs in shock,вҖқ George told Harry quietly. вҖңThat Ravenclaw girl вҖ” Penelope Clearwater вҖ” sheвҖҷs a prefect. I donвҖҷt think he thought the monster would dare attack a prefect.вҖқ
But Harry was only half-listening. He didnвҖҷt seem to be able to get rid of the picture of Hermione, lying on the hospital bed as though carved out of stone. And if the culprit wasnвҖҷt caught soon, he was looking at a lifetime back with the Dursleys. Tom Riddle had turned Hagrid in because he was faced with the prospect of a Muggle orphanage if the school closed. Harry now knew exactly how he had felt.
вҖңWhatвҖҷre we going to do?вҖқ said Ron quietly in HarryвҖҷs ear. вҖңDвҖҷyou think they suspect Hagrid?вҖқ
вҖңWeвҖҷve got to go and talk to him,вҖқ said Harry, making up his mind. вҖңI canвҖҷt believe itвҖҷs him this time, but if he set the monster loose last time heвҖҷll know how to get inside the Chamber of Secrets, and thatвҖҷs a start.вҖқ
вҖңBut McGonagall said weвҖҷve got to stay in our tower unless weвҖҷre in class вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңI think,вҖқ said Harry, more quietly still, вҖңitвҖҷs time to get my dadвҖҷs old cloak out again.вҖқ
Harry had inherited just one thing from his father: a long and silВӯvery Invisibility Cloak. It was their only chance of sneaking out of the school to visit Hagrid without anyone knowing about it. They went to bed at the usual time, waited until Neville, Dean, and SeaВӯmus had stopped discussing the Chamber of Secrets and finally fallen asleep, then got up, dressed again, and threw the cloak over themselves.
The journey through the dark and deserted castle corridors wasnвҖҷt enjoyable. Harry, who had wandered the castle at night sevВӯeral times before, had never seen it so crowded after sunset. TeachВӯers, prefects, and ghosts were marching the corridors in pairs, staring around for any unusual activity. Their Invisibility Cloak didnвҖҷt stop them making any noise, and there was a particularly tense moment when Ron stubbed his toe only yards from the spot where Snape stood standing guard. Thankfully, Snape sneezed at almost exactly the moment Ron swore. It was with relief that they reached the oak front doors and eased them open.
It was a clear, starry night. They hurried toward the lit windows of HagridвҖҷs house and pulled off the cloak only when they were right outside his front door.
Seconds after they had knocked, Hagrid flung it open. They found themselves face-to-face with him aiming a crossbow at them. Fang the boarhound barked loudly behind him.
вҖңOh,вҖқ he said, lowering the weapon and staring at them. вҖңWhatвҖҷre you two doinвҖҷ here?вҖқ
вҖңWhatвҖҷs that for?вҖқ said Harry, pointing at the crossbow as they stepped inside.
вҖңNothinвҖҷ вҖ” nothinвҖҷ вҖ” вҖң Hagrid muttered. вҖңIвҖҷve bin expectinвҖҷ вҖ” doesnвҖҷ matter вҖ” Sit down вҖ” IвҖҷll make tea вҖ”вҖқ
He hardly seemed to know what he was doing. He nearly extinВӯguished the fire, spilling water from the kettle on it, and then smashed the teapot with a nervous jerk of his massive hand.
вҖңAre you okay, Hagrid?вҖқ said Harry. вҖңDid you hear about Hermione?вҖқ
вҖңOh, I heard, all righвҖҷ,вҖқ said Hagrid, a slight break in his voice.
He kept glancing nervously at the windows. He poured them both large mugs of boiling water (he had forgotten to add tea bags) and was just putting a slab of fruitcake on a plate when there was a loud knock on the door.
Hagrid dropped the fruitcake. Harry and Ron exchanged panic-stricken looks, then threw the Invisibility Cloak back over themВӯselves and retreated into a corner. Hagrid checked that they were hidden, seized his crossbow, and flung open his door once more.
вҖңGood evening, Hagrid.вҖқ
It was Dumbledore. He entered, looking deadly serious, and was followed by a second, very odd-looking man.
The stranger had rumpled gray hair and an anxious expression, and was wearing a strange mixture of clothes: a pinstriped suit, a scarlet tie, a long black cloak, and pointed purple boots. Under his arm he carried a lime-green bowler.
вҖңThatвҖҷs DadвҖҷs boss!вҖқ Ron breathed. вҖңCornelius Fudge, the MinВӯister of Magic!вҖқ
Harry elbowed Ron hard to make him shut up.
Hagrid had gone pale and sweaty. He dropped into one of his chairs and looked from Dumbledore to Cornelius Fudge.
вҖңBad business, Hagrid,вҖқ said Fudge in rather clipped tones. вҖңVery bad business. Had to come. Four attacks on Muggle-borns. ThingsвҖҷve gone far enough. MinistryвҖҷs got to act.вҖқ
вҖңI never,вҖқ said Hagrid, looking imploringly at Dumbledore. вҖңYou know I never, Professor Dumbledore, sir вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңI want it understood, Cornelius, that Hagrid has my full confiВӯdence,вҖқ said Dumbledore, frowning at Fudge.
вҖңLook, Albus,вҖқ said Fudge, uncomfortably. вҖңHagridвҖҷs recordвҖҷs against him. MinistryвҖҷs got to do something вҖ” the school goverВӯnors have been in touch вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңYet again, Cornelius, I tell you that taking Hagrid away will not help in the slightest,вҖқ said Dumbledore. His blue eyes were full of a fire Harry had never seen before.
вҖңLook at it from my point of view,вҖқ said Fudge, fidgeting with his bowler. вҖңIвҖҷm under a lot of pressure. Got to be seen to be doing someВӯthing. If it turns out it wasnвҖҷt Hagrid, heвҖҷll be back and no more said. But IвҖҷve got to take him. Got to. WouldnвҖҷt be doing my duty вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңTake me?вҖқ said Hagrid, who was trembling. вҖңTake me where?вҖқ
вҖңFor a short stretch only,вҖқ said Fudge, not meeting HagridвҖҷs eyes. вҖңNot a punishment, Hagrid, more a precaution. If someone else is caught, youвҖҷll be let out with a full apology вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңNot Azkaban?вҖқ croaked Hagrid.
Before Fudge could answer, there was another loud rap on the door.
Dumbledore answered it. It was HarryвҖҷs turn for an elbow in the ribs; heвҖҷd let out an audible gasp.
Mr. Lucius Malfoy strode into HagridвҖҷs hut, swathed in a long black traveling cloak, smiling a cold and satisfied smile. Fang started to growl.
вҖңAlready here, Fudge,вҖқ he said approvingly. вҖңGood, good вҖҰвҖқ
вҖңWhatвҖҷre you doinвҖҷ here?вҖқ said Hagrid furiously. вҖңGet outta my house!вҖқ
вҖңMy dear man, please believe me, I have no pleasure at all in beВӯing inside your вҖ” er вҖ” dвҖҷyou call this a house?вҖқ said Lucius MalВӯfoy, sneering as he looked around the small cabin. вҖңI simply called at the school and was told that the headmaster was here.вҖқ
вҖңAnd what exactly did you want with me, Lucius?вҖқ said DumВӯbledore. He spoke politely, but the fire was still blazing in his blue eyes.
вҖңDreadful thing, Dumbledore,вҖқ said Malfoy lazily, taking out a long roll of parchment, вҖңbut the governors feel itвҖҷs time for you to step aside. This is an Order of Suspension вҖ” youвҖҷll find all twelve signatures on it. IвҖҷm afraid we feel youвҖҷre losing your touch. How many attacks have there been now? Two more this afternoon, wasnвҖҷt it? At this rate, thereвҖҷll be no Muggle-borns left at Hogwarts, and we all know what an awful loss that would be to the school.вҖқ
вҖңOh, now, see here, Lucius,вҖқ said Fudge, looking alarmed, вҖңDumbledore suspended вҖ” no, no вҖ” last thing we want just now вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңThe appointment вҖ” or suspension вҖ” of the headmaster is a matter for the governors, Fudge,вҖқ said Mr. Malfoy smoothly. вҖңAnd as Dumbledore has failed to stop these attacks вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңSee here, Malfoy, if Dumbledore canвҖҷt stop them,вҖқ said Fudge, whose upper lip was sweating now, вҖңI mean to say, who can?вҖқ
вҖңThat remains to be seen,вҖқ said Mr. Malfoy with a nasty smile. вҖңBut as all twelve of us have voted вҖ”вҖқ
Hagrid leapt to his feet, his shaggy black head grazing the ceilВӯing.
вҖңAnвҖҷ how many did yeh have ter threaten anвҖҷ blackmail before they agreed, Malfoy, eh?вҖқ he roared.
вҖңDear, dear, you know, that temper of yours will lead you into trouble one of these days, Hagrid,вҖқ said Mr. Malfoy. вҖңI would adВӯvise you not to shout at the Azkaban guards like that. They wonвҖҷt like it at all.вҖқ
вҖңYeh canвҖҷ take Dumbledore!вҖқ yelled Hagrid, making Fang the boarhound cower and whimper in his basket. вҖңTake him away, anвҖҷ the Muggle-borns wonвҖҷ stand a chance! ThereвҖҷll be killinвҖҷ next!вҖқ
вҖңCalm yourself, Hagrid,вҖқ said Dumbledore sharply. He looked at Lucius Malfoy.
вҖңIf the governors want my removal, Lucius, I shall of course step aside вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңBut вҖ”вҖқ stuttered Fudge.
вҖңNo!вҖқ growled Hagrid.
Dumbledore had not taken his bright blue eyes off Lucius MalВӯfoyвҖҷs cold gray ones.
вҖңHowever,вҖқ said Dumbledore, speaking very slowly and clearly so that none of them could miss a word, вҖңyou will find that I will only truly have left this school when none here are loyal to me. You will also find that help will always be given at Hogwarts to those who ask for it.вҖқ
For a second, Harry was almost sure DumbledoreвҖҷs eyes flickered toward the corner where he and Ron stood hidden.
вҖңAdmirable sentiments,вҖқ said Malfoy, bowing. вҖңWe shall all miss your вҖ” er вҖ” highly individual way of running things, Albus, and only hope that your successor will manage to prevent any вҖ” ah вҖ” killins.вҖқ
He strode to the cabin door, opened it, and bowed Dumbledore out. Fudge, fiddling with his bowler, waited for Hagrid to go ahead of him, but Hagrid stood his ground, took a deep breath, and said carefully, вҖңIf anyone wanted ter find out some stuff, all theyвҖҷd have ter do would be ter follow the spiders. ThatвҖҷd lead вҖҷem right! ThatвҖҷs all IвҖҷm sayinвҖҷ.вҖқ
Fudge stared at him in amazement.
вҖңAll right, IвҖҷm cominвҖҷ,вҖқ said Hagrid, pulling on his moleskin overcoat. But as he was about to follow Fudge through the door, he stopped again and said loudly, вҖңAnвҖҷ someoneвҖҷll need ter feed Fang while IвҖҷm away.вҖқ
The door banged shut and Ron pulled off the Invisibility Cloak.
вҖңWeвҖҷre in trouble now,вҖқ he said hoarsely. вҖңNo Dumbledore. They might as well close the school tonight. ThereвҖҷll be an attack a day with him gone.вҖқ
Fang started howling, scratching at the closed door.
## Chapter 15

Aragog
Summer was creeping over the grounds around the castle; sky and lake alike turned periwinkle blue and flowers large as cabВӯbages burst into bloom in the greenhouses. But with no Hagrid visВӯible from the castle windows, striding the grounds with Fang at his heels, the scene didnвҖҷt look right to Harry; no better, in fact, than the inside of the castle, where things were so horribly wrong.
Harry and Ron had tried to visit Hermione, but visitors were now barred from the hospital wing.
вҖңWeвҖҷre taking no more chances,вҖқ Madam Pomfrey told them seВӯverely through a crack in the infirmary door. вҖңNo, IвҖҷm sorry, thereвҖҷs every chance the attacker might come back to finish these people off. вҖҰвҖқ
With Dumbledore gone, fear had spread as never before, so that the sun warming the castle walls outside seemed to stop at the mulВӯlioned windows. There was barely a face to be seen in the school that didnвҖҷt look worried and tense, and any laughter that rang through the corridors sounded shrill and unnatural and was quickly stifled.
Harry constantly repeated DumbledoreвҖҷs final words to himself. вҖңI will only truly have left this school when none here are loyal to me. вҖҰ Help will always be given at Hogwarts to those who ask for it.вҖқ But what good were these words? Who exactly were they supВӯposed to ask for help, when everyone was just as confused and scared as they were?
HagridвҖҷs hint about the spiders was far easier to understand вҖ” the trouble was, there didnвҖҷt seem to be a single spider left in the castle to follow. Harry looked everywhere he went, helped (rather reluctantly) by Ron. They were hampered, of course, by the fact that they werenвҖҷt allowed to wander off on their own but had to move around the castle in a pack with the other Gryffindors. Most of their fellow students seemed glad that they were being shepВӯherded from class to class by teachers, but Harry found it very irkВӯsome.
One person, however, seemed to be thoroughly enjoying the atВӯmosphere of terror and suspicion. Draco Malfoy was strutting around the school as though he had just been appointed Head Boy. Harry didnвҖҷt realize what he was so pleased about until the Potions lesson about two weeks after Dumbledore and Hagrid had left, when, sitting right behind Malfoy, Harry overheard him gloating to Crabbe and Goyle.
вҖңI always thought Father might be the one who got rid of DumВӯbledore,вҖқ he said, not troubling to keep his voice down. вҖңI told you he thinks DumbledoreвҖҷs the worst headmaster the schoolвҖҷs ever had. Maybe weвҖҷll get a decent headmaster now. Someone who wonвҖҷt want the Chamber of Secrets closed. McGonagall wonвҖҷt last long, sheвҖҷs only filling in. вҖҰвҖқ
Snape swept past Harry, making no comment about HermioneвҖҷs empty seat and cauldron.
вҖңSir,вҖқ said Malfoy loudly. вҖңSir, why donвҖҷt you apply for the headВӯmasterвҖҷs job?вҖқ
вҖңNow, now, Malfoy,вҖқ said Snape, though he couldnвҖҷt suppress a thin-lipped smile. вҖңProfessor Dumbledore has only been suspended by the governors. I daresay heвҖҷll be back with us soon enough.вҖқ
вҖңYeah, right,вҖқ said Malfoy, smirking. вҖңI expect youвҖҷd have FaВӯtherвҖҷs vote, sir, if you wanted to apply for the job вҖ” IвҖҷll tell Father youвҖҷre the best teacher here, sir вҖ”вҖқ
Snape smirked as he swept off around the dungeon, fortunately not spotting Seamus Finnigan, who was pretending to vomit into his cauldron.
вҖңIвҖҷm quite surprised the Mudbloods havenвҖҷt all packed their bags by now,вҖқ Malfoy went on. вҖңBet you five Galleons the next one dies. Pity it wasnвҖҷt Granger вҖ”вҖқ
The bell rang at that moment, which was lucky; at MalfoyвҖҷs last words, Ron had leapt off his stool, and in the scramble to collect bags and books, his attempts to reach Malfoy went unnoticed.
вҖңLet me at him,вҖқ Ron growled as Harry and Dean hung onto his arms. вҖңI donвҖҷt care, I donвҖҷt need my wand, IвҖҷm going to kill him with my bare hands вҖ”вҖқ
вҖңHurry up, IвҖҷve got to take you all to Herbology,вҖқ barked Snape over the classвҖҷs heads, and off they marched, with Harry, Ron, and Dean bringing up the rear, Ron still trying to get loose. It was only safe to let go of him when Snape had seen them out of the castle and they were making their way across the vegetable patch toward the greenhouses.
The Herbology class was very subdued; there were now two missing from their number, Justin and Hermione.
Professor Sprout set them all to work pruning the Abyssinian Shrivelfigs. Harry went to tip an armful of withered stalks onto the compost heap and found himself face-to-face with Ernie MacmilВӯlan. Ernie took a deep breath and said, very formally, вҖңI just want to say, Harry, that IвҖҷm sorry I ever suspected you. I know youвҖҷd never attack Hermione Granger, and I apologize for all the stuff I said. WeвҖҷre all in the same boat now, and, well вҖ”вҖқ
He held out a pudgy hand, and Harry shook it.
Ernie and his friend Hannah came to work at the same Shrivelfig as Harry and Ron.
вҖңThat Draco Malfoy character,вҖқ said Ernie, breaking off dead twigs, вҖңhe seems very pleased about all this, doesnвҖҷt he? DвҖҷyou know, I think he might be SlytherinвҖҷs heir.вҖқ
вҖңThatвҖҷs clever of you,вҖқ said Ron, who didnвҖҷt seem to have forВӯgiven Ernie as readily as Harry.
вҖңDo you think itвҖҷs Malfoy, Harry?вҖқ Ernie asked.
вҖңNo,вҖқ said Harry, so firmly that Ernie and Hannah stared.
A second later, Harry spotted something.
Several large spiders were scuttling over the ground on the other side of the glass, moving in an unnaturally straight line as though taking the shortest route to a prearranged meeting. Harry hit Ron over the hand with his pruning shears.
вҖңOuch! WhatвҖҷre you вҖ”вҖқ
Harry pointed out the spiders, following their progress with his eyes screwed up against the sun.
вҖңOh, yeah,вҖқ said Ron, trying, and failing, to look pleased. вҖңBut we canвҖҷt follow them now вҖ”вҖқ
Ernie and Hannah were listening curiously.
